// Function Class: Show/Hide product promotions & special offers link
// =============================================================================

function showElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'visible';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'block';
    }
  }
}
function hideElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }
}
function showHideElement(h_id, div_id) {
  var hiddenTag = document.getElementById(h_id);
  if (hiddenTag) {
    showElement(div_id);
  } else {
    hideElement(div_id);
  }
}

    // Logic to Control When BBOP is Loaded
    if( window.P ){
        P.when("A").execute(function(A) {

                window.sbbopLoaded = false;

            function getQueryParameterByName(name) {
              name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");

              var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
                  results = regex.exec(location.search);

              return results == null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
            }

            // Cross-Browser Visibility API
            var hidden, visibilityChange;
            if (typeof document.hidden !== "undefined") { // Opera 12.10 and Firefox 18 and later support
                hidden = "hidden";
                  visibilityChange = "visibilitychange";
            } else if (typeof document.mozHidden !== "undefined") {
                  hidden = "mozHidden";
                  visibilityChange = "mozvisibilitychange";
            } else if (typeof document.msHidden !== "undefined") {
                  hidden = "msHidden";
                  visibilityChange = "msvisibilitychange";
            } else if (typeof document.webkitHidden !== "undefined") {
                  hidden = "webkitHidden";
                  visibilityChange = "webkitvisibilitychange";
            }
            
            // Core Features Logic
            var loadFeatures = function() {
                
                

                var $ = A.$,
                    $container = $("#bbop-sbbop-container"),
                    embuSbbopEventId = 106,
                    metricsScope = "surpriseBBOP",
                    deliveryOptions = "[std-us, next, sss-us]",
                    preorder = "false",
                    releaseDateDeliveryEligible = "false",
                    bbopRuleIdString = "Acquisition_AddToCart_PrimeBasicFreeTrialUpsellEligible",
                    sbbopRuleIdString = "Acquisition_AddToCart_PrimeBasicFreeTrialUpsellEligible";

                var data = {
                    "ASIN" : "B001RG7LDU",
                    "merchantID" : "ATVPDKIKX0DER",
                    "bbopruleID" : bbopRuleIdString,
                    "sbbopruleID" : sbbopRuleIdString,
                    "deliveryOptions" : deliveryOptions,
                    "preorder" : preorder,
                    "releaseDateDeliveryEligible" : releaseDateDeliveryEligible
                };
                $.get("/gp/product/du/bbop-ms3-ajax-endpoint.html", data, function(result) {     
                    $container.append(result);

                    if (getQueryParameterByName("checkBBOP") === "true") {
                        P.when("a-modal", "ready").execute(function(modal) {
                          $('#bbop-check-box').click();
                        });
                    }
                    
                    loadSBBOP();
                    
                });

                
                var loadSBBOP = function(){
                    P.when("a-modal", "ready").execute(function(modal) {
                        if(!window.sbbopLoaded){
                            var sbbop_modal = createModal(modal);

                            if (sbbop_modal !== undefined) {
                                $(document.body).delegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.sbbop', function(event){
                                    $(document.body).undelegate('#add-to-cart-button','click.sbbop');

                                    var $sbbop = $("#sbbop-container"),
                                        $sbbopContent = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-content"),
                                        $sbbopHeader = $container.find("#sbbop-popover-header"),
                                        $sbbopFooter = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-footer"),
                                        $atcButton = $('#add-to-cart-button'),
                                        atcName = $atcButton.attr("name"),
                                        hasSingleYesButton = ($('#sbbop-yes-button').length === 1),
                                        hasSingleNoButton  = ($('#sbbop-no-button').length === 1),
                                        validAtcButton = ($atcButton.length === 1 && atcName != "submit.add-to-cart-prime-buy-box.x"),
                                        validSbbopContent = ($sbbopContent.length === 1 && $sbbopHeader.length === 1 && $sbbopFooter.length === 1),
                                        validSbbopButtons = (hasSingleYesButton && hasSingleNoButton);

                                    if(validAtcButton && validSbbopContent && validSbbopButtons){
                                        $atcButton.bind('click.sbbop', function(){return false;});  
                                        $(document.body).delegate("#sbbop-yes-button", "click", function(event){
                                            $atcButton.attr("name", "submit.add-to-cart-prime-buy-box.x");
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_yes_button");
                                            safeATCClick();
                                        });

                                        $(document.body).delegate("#sbbop-no-button", "click", function(event){
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_no_button");
                                            safeATCClick();
                                        });

                                        A.on("a:popover:ajaxFail:sbbop_modal", safeATCClick);
                                        A.on("a:popover:hide:sbbop_modal", function(){
                                            logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_close_button");
                                            safeATCClick();
                                        });
                                        A.on("a:popover:beforeShow:sbbop_modal", function(){
                                        
                                            
                                                recordEmbuAndTriggerWeblab();                
                                            
                                            
                                                 
                                        });

                                        sbbop_modal.show();
                                        logMetric("CSM_prime_surprise_BBOP_presentation");
                                        return false;
                                    } else if (validAtcButton && validSbbopContent){
                                        
                                           $atcButton.bind('click.sbbop', function(){return false;});  
                                           triggerWeblab();
                                           return false;
                                        
                                        
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                            window.sbbopLoaded = true;
                        }
                    });
                };

                var createModal = function(modal) {
                    var $sbbop = $("#sbbop-container"),
                        $sbbopContent = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-content"),
                        $sbbopHeader = $container.find("#sbbop-popover-header"),
                        $sbbopFooter = $sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover-footer");

                    if($sbbopContent.length === 1 && $sbbopHeader.length === 1 && $sbbopFooter.length === 1){ 
                        sbbopWidth = parseInt(($sbbop.find("#sbbop-popover")).attr("popover-width"), 10);
                    
                        return modal.create($sbbop, {
                            "inlineContent": $sbbopContent.html(),
                            "header": $sbbopHeader.html(),
                            "footer": $sbbopFooter.html(),
                            "width": sbbopWidth,
                            "activate": "onclick",
                            "name": "sbbop_modal"
                        });
                    }
                    return undefined;
                }
                
                var logMetric = function(customTag){
                    if(window.ue && ue.tag) {
                        ue.tag(customTag, metricsScope)
                    }
                };

                var postBackMetrics = function(){
                    if (window.ue){
                        uex( "ld", metricsScope );
                    }
                };

                var setEventEmbu = function(){
                    var eventData = { "eventCode" : embuSbbopEventId };
                    $.get("/gp/prime/utility/record-embu-event.html", eventData);
                };

                var recordEmbuAndTriggerWeblab = function(){
                    var requestData = { "requestType" : "RECORD_EMBU" };
                    $.get("/gp/product/du/sbbop-ajax-endpoint.html", requestData);
                };
               
                var triggerWeblab = function(){
                    $.get("/gp/product/du/sbbop-ajax-endpoint.html")
                        .always(function() {
                            safeATCClick();
                        });                  
                 }

                var safeATCClick = function() {
                    postBackMetrics();                                               
                    $('#add-to-cart-button').unbind('click.sbbop')                   
                        .click()                                                     
                        .bind('click.sbbop',function(){return false});               
                };
                
                
            }

            // Event to be fired if BBOP is not displayed and page becomes visible
            var handleVisibilityChange = function() {
                if (!document[hidden]) {
                    // Only load BBOP once
                    document.removeEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);
                    loadFeatures();
                }
            }

            if (typeof document.addEventListener === "undefined" ||
                typeof document[hidden] === "undefined" || !document[hidden]) {
                // If page is visible or visibility API unsupported, do BBOP now
                loadFeatures();
            } else {
                // If page is not visible, listen for visibility change to display BBOP
                document.addEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);
            }
        });
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
maintainHeight = function(){
    var mainHolder = document.getElementById("main-image-container");
    var imgTagWrapperId = document.getElementById("imgTagWrapperId");
    if(mainHolder && typeof mainHolder != 'undefined'){
        var width = mainHolder.offsetWidth;
        var ratio = 0.84;
        var shouldAutoPlay = false;
        var videoSizes = [[342, 69], [385, 77], [425, 85], [466, 94], [522, 105]];
        
        var containerHeight = width/ratio;
        containerHeight = Math.min(containerHeight, 700);
        mainHolder.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
        if(imgTagWrapperId && typeof imgTagWrapperId !== 'undefined' ){
            imgTagWrapperId.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
        }

        var landingImage = document.getElementById("landingImage");
        var imageHeight = Math.min(containerHeight, 105);
        var imageWidth = Math.min(width, 522);
        if(landingImage){
            landingImage.style.maxHeight = imageHeight + "px";
            landingImage.style.maxWidth  = imageWidth + "px";
        }
        
        if(shouldAutoPlay){
            if(landingImage){
                var autoPlayWidth=0, autoPlayHeight=0;
                for(var i=0; i < videoSizes.length; i++){
                    if( autoPlayWidth < videoSizes[i][0] ){
                        autoPlayWidth = videoSizes[i][0];
                        autoPlayHeight = videoSizes[i][1];
                    }
                }
                if( autoPlayWidth > 0 && autoPlayHeight > 0 ){
                    var videoRatio = autoPlayWidth/autoPlayHeight;
                    // increasing height of the slate image by 1px (and width with the ratio) so that black lines doesn't appear on ipad on right side.
                    var isIpad = navigator.userAgent.match(/ipad/i);
                    if( isIpad ){
                        containerHeight = containerHeight + 1;
                    }
                    landingImage.style.width = containerHeight * videoRatio + "px";
                    landingImage.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
                }
                
            }
        }
    }
};
maintainHeight();

window.onresize = function(){
    maintainHeight();
};

<script type="text/javascript">
FT_showAndInCountdown = false;
FT_HourString = "hr";
FT_HoursString = "hrs";
FT_MinuteString = "min";
FT_MinutesString = "mins";
FT_AndString = "and";

function getElementsByClassNameCustom(className) {
    var selectedElements = [];
    if (document.getElementsByClassName) {
        selectedElements = document.getElementsByClassName(className);
    } else if (document.querySelectorAll) {
        selectedElements = document.querySelectorAll("." + className);
    }
    return selectedElements;
}

var FT_CurrentDisplayMin;
var clientServerTimeDrift;
var firstTimeUpdate = true;

var countdownElements = getElementsByClassNameCustom("ftCountdownClass");
if (countdownElements.length < 1) {
    countdownElements.push(document.getElementById("ftCountdown"));
}

function getTimeRemainingString( hours, minutes )
{
  var hourString   =  ( hours == 1 ? FT_HourString : FT_HoursString );
  var minuteString =  ( minutes  == 1 ? FT_MinuteString : FT_MinutesString );
  if (hours == 0) {
    return minutes + " " + minuteString;
  }
  if (minutes == 0) {
    return hours + " " + hourString;
  }
  if (FT_showAndInCountdown) {
    return hours + " " + hourString + " " + FT_AndString + " " + minutes + " " + minuteString;
  } else {
    return hours + " " + hourString + " " + minutes + " " + minuteString;
  }
}
function FT_displayCountdown(forceUpdate)
{
  var FT_remainSeconds = FT_givenSeconds - FT_actualSeconds;
  if (FT_remainSeconds < 1 && document.getElementById("fast-track")) {
    document.getElementById("fast-track").style.display = "none";
  }
  var FT_secondsPerDay = 24 * 60 * 60;
  var FT_daysLong = FT_remainSeconds / FT_secondsPerDay;
  var FT_days = Math.floor(FT_daysLong);
  var FT_hoursLong = (FT_daysLong - FT_days) * 24;
  var FT_hours = Math.floor(FT_hoursLong);
  var FT_minsLong = (FT_hoursLong - FT_hours) * 60;
  var FT_mins = Math.floor(FT_minsLong);
  var FT_secsLong = (FT_minsLong - FT_mins) * 60;
  var FT_secs = Math.floor(FT_secsLong);
  if (FT_days > 0) {
    FT_hours = (FT_days * 24) + FT_hours;
  }
  setTimeout(FT_getTime, 1000);
  var ftCountdown = getTimeRemainingString( FT_hours, FT_mins );
  if (countdownElements.length) {
    if (FT_CurrentDisplayMin != FT_mins || forceUpdate || firstTimeUpdate) {
      var i = 0, countdownElement;
      while (countdownElement = countdownElements[i++]) {
        countdownElement.innerHTML = ftCountdown;
      }
      FT_CurrentDisplayMin = FT_mins;
      firstTimeUpdate = false;
    }
  }
}

function FT_getCountdown(secondsLeft)
{
  var FT_currentTime = new Date();
  var FT_currentHours = FT_currentTime.getHours();
  var FT_currentMins = FT_currentTime.getMinutes();
  var FT_currentSecs = FT_currentTime.getSeconds();
  FT_givenSeconds = FT_currentHours * 3600 + FT_currentMins * 60 + FT_currentSecs;
  FT_givenSeconds += secondsLeft;
  FT_getTime();
}
function FT_getTime()
{
  var FT_newCurrentTime = new Date();
  var FT_actualHours = FT_newCurrentTime.getHours();
  var FT_actualMins = FT_newCurrentTime.getMinutes();
  var FT_actualSecs = FT_newCurrentTime.getSeconds();
  FT_actualSeconds = FT_actualHours * 3600 + FT_actualMins * 60 + FT_actualSecs;
  FT_displayCountdown();
}
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            FT_getCountdown(8184);
        </script>
    
</div>

        
        <script type="text/javascript">
    P.when("A", "jQuery").execute(function(A, $) {
        $("#quantity").live("change", function (event) {
            if (event.updateFTOnQuantityChange) {
                return;
            }
            event.updateFTOnQuantityChange = 1;

            var quantity = $(this).val();
            var asin = $("#ftSelectAsin").val();
            var merchantId = $("#ftSelectMerchant").val();

            if (!asin || !merchantId) {
                return;
            }

            var params = [];
            params.push("asin=" + asin);
            params.push("quantity=" + quantity);
            params.push("merchantId=" + merchantId);

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/gp/product/features/dp-fast-track/udp-ajax-handler/get-quantity-update-message.html?ie=UTF8",
                contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8',
                data: params.join('&'),
                dataType: "html",
                success: function(objResponse) {
                    if (objResponse != null && objResponse != "") {
                        $("#fast-track-message").replaceWith(objResponse);
                    }
                }
            });
            return;
        });
    });
</script>

        function dumpHtml( obj, newAdsHtml, topHtml, bottomHtml, divParent ) {
              var i = 0;
              var completeAdsHtml = '';
              for( x in obj ) {
                  var adChunks = newAdsHtml.split( adPropertiesDelimiter );
                  for( var j = 0; j<adChunks.length; j++ ) {
                      if( typeof obj[i][adChunks[j]] != "undefined" ) {
                          adChunks[j] = obj[i][adChunks[j]];
                      }
                  }
                  completeAdsHtml += adChunks.join("");
                  i++;
              }
              newAdsHtml = topHtml + completeAdsHtml + bottomHtml;
              $('#' + divParent).replaceWith(newAdsHtml);
        }
	});

<script type="text/javascript">
var ProductDescriptionIframeResize = {};
(function () {
  var d = document;
  var obj = this;
  var nTries = 1;
  var hasCustomWidth = 0;
  var MAX_TRIES = 20;
  obj.iframeId = 'product-description-iframe';
  obj.appendTo = 'iframe-wrapper';
  function getDocHeight (doc) {
    var contentDiv = doc.getElementById("pdIframeContent");
    return Math.max(
      contentDiv.scrollHeight,
      contentDiv.offsetHeight,
      contentDiv.clientHeight
    );
  }
  function isElementOnRight(pdRef, el) {
    var ret=0;
    try {
      if(pdRef, el) {
        if((el.offsetTop < pdRef.offsetTop) && (el.offsetTop + el.offsetHeight > pdRef.offsetTop)) {
          ret = 1;
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {}
    return ret;
  }
  function setWidth(iframeRef, el) {
    var elLeft, w, minW = 450;
    try {
      elLeft = el.offsetLeft;
      w = elLeft - 50;
      if(w > minW) {
        iframeRef.style.width = w + 'px';
        hasCustomWidth = 1;
      }
    } catch (e) {}
  }
  function setIframeWidth(ifrmId) {
    var iframeRef = d.getElementById(ifrmId),
        pdRef = d.getElementById("pd-available"),
        rightCol = d.getElementById("rightCol"),
        rightRail = d.getElementById("rightRail");
    if(isElementOnRight(pdRef, rightRail)) {
      setWidth(iframeRef, rightRail); 
    } else if (isElementOnRight(pdRef, rightCol)) {
      setWidth(iframeRef, rightCol);
    }
  }
  function setIframeHeight (ifrmId) {
    var iframeDoc, iframeRef = d.getElementById(ifrmId);
    try {
      iframeDoc = iframeRef.contentWindow.document;
    } catch (e) {
      try {
        iframeDoc = iframeRef.contentDocument;
      } catch (ex) {}
    }
    if (iframeDoc) {
      var h = getDocHeight(iframeDoc);
      if (h != 0) {
        iframeRef.style.height = h + 'px';
      } else { 
        if (nTries < MAX_TRIES) {
          nTries++;
          setTimeout(function () {
            setIframeHeight(ifrmId);
          }, 50); 
        }
      }
    }
  }
  obj.iframeload = function () {
    var iframe = d.getElementById(obj.iframeId);
    iframe.style.display = '';
    iframe.style.height = "1px";
    setTimeout(function () {
      if(obj.needWidthAdjust) {
        setIframeWidth(obj.iframeId);
      }
      setIframeHeight(obj.iframeId);
      var onloadCallback = obj.onloadCallback;
      if(typeof onloadCallback === "function") {
        onloadCallback();
      }
    }, 50); 

  }
  obj.createIframe = function ( iframeId, onloadFn ) {
    var iframe = d.createElement('iframe');
    iframe.id = iframeId;
    iframe.className = "ap_never_hide";
    iframe.width = "100%";
    iframe.scrolling="no";
    iframe.frameBorder="0";
    if ( iframe.addEventListener )
      iframe.addEventListener("load", onloadFn, false);
    else if ( iframe.attachEvent )
      iframe.attachEvent("onload", onloadFn);
    else iframe.onload = onloadFn;
    return iframe; 
  }
  obj.initialize = function (onloadCallback, needWidthAdjust) {
    var iframeContent = <div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3GPXQIUUFPMA4" class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">173 of 182 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3GPXQIUUFPMA4/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/189-4296928-9782310?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001RG7LDU&nodeID=165793011&store=toys-and-games"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R3GPXQIUUFPMA4/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/189-4296928-9782310?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001RG7LDU&nodeID=165793011&store=toys-and-games"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Awesome Train For The Christmas Tree</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">






  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">

    </span>
    <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A3THC2ABFJH96G/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/189-4296928-9782310" class="noTextDecoration">Amazon Customer</a>

<div class="a-section">
  I bought this Bachmann train set to put under the Christmas tree this year.  I was thinking of getting the bigger O or G scale train, but the HO is the perfect size and I'm really glad I went with it.  The HO size has a perfectly sized track that fits under the Christmas tree without needing the typical 4'X 8' space that most larger trains need for the track. The Locomotive is the heaviest of the train pieces and most well built piece, but that's because the other train pieces just need to roll behind it.  Overall I'm really happy with the build quality, and the track was super easy to snap together.  The conductor controls are also really easy to use and my 2 year old quickly learned how to move the train forward and in reverse in a manner of minutes.  I would recommend this train to anyone looking for a train set for under the Christmas tree. Great Price, fairly quiet, and great size!<br><br>**Here is some video I took of the train to help you see how it looks and operates.  I was running the train at about 1/3 of the full speed.  The train operates and stays on the track at full speed as long as the track is completely level on the floor, or on a table.
</div>

<div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-RBMURRCCHVJJJ" class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">29 of 30 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="4.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/RBMURRCCHVJJJ/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/189-4296928-9782310?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001RG7LDU&nodeID=165793011&store=toys-and-games"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-4"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/RBMURRCCHVJJJ/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/189-4296928-9782310?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001RG7LDU&nodeID=165793011&store=toys-and-games"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">GOOD VALUE Great train set for beginners.</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">






  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
    <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/AUTJRJJOF7PK9/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/189-4296928-9782310" class="noTextDecoration">dextex</a>
  </span>
<span class="a-color-secondary"> on March 4, 2012</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-RBMURRCCHVJJJ" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">
    Verified Purchase
  </span>





<div class="a-section">
  The train arrived very promptly (Prime) and was in great shape. The cost was around $74. Store price was around $95. It only has three cars but that is enough. Our six year old grand son is able to put the track together, put the cars and train on the track and enjoys connecting the cars and running the train. It is the combination of the houses, small buildings, gas station and imagination that makes it such a fine item. He is continually changing the layout of the buildings around the track. For a few dollars you can go to the Dollar Store and buy some moss sheets that he uses as a field and some other items he was able to turn into shrubs. Its all about the imagination. This product is the melody to the harmony of creation in encouraging a young child's mind.
</div>

</div>

<div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R17F9ESKKBS27R" class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">13 of 15 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R17F9ESKKBS27R/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/189-4296928-9782310?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001RG7LDU&nodeID=165793011&store=toys-and-games"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R17F9ESKKBS27R/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/189-4296928-9782310?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B001RG7LDU&nodeID=165793011&store=toys-and-games"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Great starter set</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">






  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
    <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A3395MC78WZOSC/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/189-4296928-9782310" class="noTextDecoration">Paul T. Stowitts</a>
  </span>
<span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup="{&quot;width&quot;:340,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;AmazonHelp&quot;,&quot;height&quot;:340}" style="display:inline;"></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on June 7, 2012</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R17F9ESKKBS27R" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">
    Verified Purchase
  </span>





<div class="a-section">
  I purchased this item to use in a project for my daughter's fifth grade class.  The package arrived quickly and I had it set up in a few minutes.  The controller initially worked erratically but Bachmann sent a replacement (and a new wallpack) right away (great customer service).  I tried the original controller after I had received the replacement and it worked fine then.<br><br>The engine ran better than any other HO engine I have owned in the past.  It was smooth and never hesitated at any speed.  A sticker on the box explains why the wheels may come off from time to time but I never had any come off (even after the fifth graders got their hands on it).  Getting the cars placed properly on the track can be difficult if you try to do it by hand but one of the straight sections (looks like the rail is crossing a street) will actually "rerail" the cars when you move them back and forth over this section (the trucks must be oriented in the same direction of the track for this to work).<br><br>The class project was a demonstration of an automated controller running a train.  I added a control panel, a small controller, some sensors and LEDs to simulate controls on a real railroad.  The layout was left in the class for the kids to play with for the last four weeks.  When I picked it up today, the train still worked like a champ.
</div>

</div>

      }
    };

<script type="text/JavaScript">

window.rhf_use_AUI = 1 && typeof P === 'object' && P.AUI_BUILD_DATE;


window.rhf_use_AUI_lib = typeof P === 'object' && P.AUI_BUILD_DATE;

if (!window.rhf_use_AUI_lib) {
    

amznJQ.addLogical('p13nlogger', ['http://z-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/browser-scripts/p13nlogger/p13nlogger-3861958816._V1_.js']);
amznJQ.addLogical('callOnVisible', ['http://z-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/browser-scripts/callOnVisible/callOnVisible-66186444._V1_.js']);

var rhfP13NLogger = function(rhfWaitTime, success) {
    amznJQ.onReady('callOnVisible', function () {        
        var rhfContainer = jQuery("#rhf_container");
        var action = success ? 'view' : 'ajax_failure';
       	if (typeof rhfContainer.callOnVisible == 'function') {
	    rhfContainer.callOnVisible(function () {
                var rhfLog = function(eventData) {
		    amznJQ.onReady('p13nlogger', function() {
			var commonData = {
		            channel: 'recommendations',
			    widget: 'pd_rhf',
			    featureElement: rhfContainer,
			    requestInfoElement: '#rhf0RequestInfo'
			};
			p13n.logEvent(jQuery.extend({}, commonData, eventData));
		    });
		};
		rhfLog({
		   action: action,
		   page: 1,
		   eventtime: rhfWaitTime,
		   meta: {'isRHFLoaded': success}
		});
	    }, 0); 
        }
    });
};

var rhfRVIP13NLogger = function() {
        var rviContainer = jQuery("#horizontal-list");
        var shvlContainer = jQuery('#rhf_upsell_div');
        var isEventComplete = function() {
            return shvlContainer.find('.rhf_loading_outer').size() == 0;
        };
        var rviLog = function(eventData) {
            amznJQ.onReady('p13nlogger', function() {
               var commonData = {
                   channel: 'recommendations',
                   widget: 'pd_rhf',
                   isEventComplete: isEventComplete,
                   featureElement: shvlContainer,
                   requestInfoElement: '#rhf0RequestInfo'
               };
              p13n.logAsyncEvent(jQuery.extend({}, commonData, eventData));
            });
        };
        rviContainer.find('.rhf-RVIs').click(function() {
            rviLog({
                action: 'rvi_click',
                page: 1
            });
        });
        rviContainer.find('.clearSelection').click(function() {
            rviLog({
                action: 'clear_click',
                page: 1 
            }); 
        });
};

}

var rhfShovelerBootstrapFunction = function($) { (function($) {

    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = false;
    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = false;
    window.RECS_rhfInView = false;
    window.RECS_rhfMetrics = {};

    var rhfWaitTime = 0;

    $("#rhf_container").show();
    var rhfShvlEventHandler = function () {
        if (   ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded
            && ! window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading
            && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0 ) {
            var yPosition = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
            var rhfElementFound = $('#rhfMainHeading').size();
            var rhfPosition = $('#rhfMainHeading').offset().top;

            if (/webkit.*mobile/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                rhfPosition -= $(window).scrollTop();
            }

            if (rhfElementFound && ( rhfPosition - yPosition < 400 )) {
                window.RECS_rhfMetrics["start"] = (new Date()).getTime();
                window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading = true;
                var handleSuccess = function (html) {
                    $("#rhf_container").html(html);
                    $("#rhf0Shvl").trigger("render-shoveler");
                    window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded = true;
                    window.RECS_rhfMetrics["loaded"] = (new Date()).getTime();
                    if (!window.rhf_use_AUI_lib) {
                        rhfWaitTime = window.RECS_rhfMetrics["loaded"] - window.RECS_rhfMetrics["inView"];
                        rhfP13NLogger(rhfWaitTime, true);
                        rhfRVIP13NLogger();
                    }
                    //If RHF is loaded, remove the interval.
                    if ("C" === "T1" && window.rhf_trigger_event) {
                        clearInterval(window.rhf_trigger_event);
                    }
                };
                var handleError = function () {
                    $("#rhf_container").hide();
                    $("#rhf_error").show();
                    window.RECS_rhfMetrics["loaded"] = "error";
                    if (!window.rhf_use_AUI_lib) {
                        rhfP13NLogger(rhfWaitTime, false);
                    }
                    //If RHF fails to load, remove the interval.
                    if ("C" === "T1" && window.rhf_trigger_event) {
                        clearInterval(window.rhf_trigger_event);
                    }
                };
                var ajaxURL = '/gp/history/external/full-rhf-rec-handler.html/189-4296928-9782310';
                var ajaxArgs = {
                    type: "POST",
                    timeout: 10000,
                    data: {
                        shovelerName    : 'rhf0',
                        key             : 'rhf',
                        numToPreload    : '8',
                        isGateway       : 0,
                        refTag          : 'pd_rhf_dp',
                        parentSession   : '189-4296928-9782310',
                        relatedRequestId: '1GWSDKAKHAY28GM1SD53',
                        excludeASIN     : 'B001RG7LDU',
                        renderPopover   : 0,
                        forceSprites    : 1,
                        currentPageType : 'Detail',
                        currentSubPageType : 'Glance',
                        weblabTriggers  : "",
                        // We'll pretend that AUI is disabled everywhere until all AUI carousel bugs are fixed.
                        isAUI           : window.rhf_use_AUI ? 1 : 0
                    },
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function (data, status) {
                        if (typeof(data) === 'object' && data.success && data.html) {
                            handleSuccess(data.html);
                            if (window.rhf_use_AUI) {
                                P.when("jQuery", "a-carousel-framework").execute(function(jQuery, framework){
                                  jQuery("#rhf_upsell_div .a-carousel-viewport").addClass("a-carousel-slide");
                                  framework.createAll();
                                });
                            }
                        } else {
                            handleError();
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (xhr, status) {
                        handleError();
                    }
                };
                if (window.rhf_use_AUI) {
                    P.when("A").execute(function (A) {
                        A.$.ajax(ajaxURL, ajaxArgs);
                    });
                } else {
                    ajaxArgs['url'] = ajaxURL;
                    $.ajax(ajaxArgs);
                }
            }
        }
    };
    var getDuplicateASINList = function() {
        var cartRecsASINList;
        if (window.rhf_use_AUI) {
            var cartCarouselParams = $("div[data-p13n-widget = 'pd_cart_recs']").attr("data-a-carousel-options");
            if (cartCarouselParams) {
                cartRecsASINList = JSON.parse(cartCarouselParams).ajax.id_list;
                //Get first 10 of the List, will get all of them if less than 10
                return JSON.stringify(cartRecsASINList.slice(0, 10));
            }
        } else if (window.RECS_cartRecs_ASINList) {
            cartRecsASINList = window.RECS_cartRecs_ASINList;
            return JSON.stringify(cartRecsASINList.slice(0, 10));
        }
        return cartRecsASINList;
    };
    var rhfInView = function() {
        if (!window.RECS_rhfInView && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0) {
            var yPosition = $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
            var rhfElementFound = ($('#rhfMainHeading').size() > 0);
            var rhfPosition = $('#rhfMainHeading').offset().top;
            if (/webkit.*mobile/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                rhfPosition -= $(window).scrollTop();
            }
            if (rhfElementFound && ( rhfPosition - yPosition < 0 )) {
                window.RECS_rhfInView = true;
                window.RECS_rhfMetrics["inView"] = (new Date()).getTime();
                if ("C" === "T1" && window.rhf_inView_event) {
                    clearInterval(window.rhf_inView_event);
                }
            }
        }
    };
    window.rhfYBHTurnOn = function () {
            $.ajax({
                  url: '/gp/history/external/full-rhf-ybh-on-handler.html/189-4296928-9782310',
                  type: "POST",
                  timeout: 2000,
                  data: {
                         parentSession    : '189-4296928-9782310'
                  },
                  dataType: "text",
                  success: function (data, status) {
                               $("#yourBrowsingHistoryOnText").find('p').html("You don't have any recently viewed Items.");
                               $("#rhf-ybh-turn-on-link").hide();
                  }
            });
    };
    $(document).ready(rhfShvlEventHandler);
    $(document).ready(rhfInView);

    if ("C" === "T1") {
        //We met some problems with jQuery scroll function, so we decide to use setInterval for checking RHF triggering status.
        //https://tt.amazon.com/0026187346
        window.rhf_trigger_event = setInterval(function () {
            if (!window.RECS_rhfShvlLoaded
                && !window.RECS_rhfShvlLoading
                && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0) {
                rhfShvlEventHandler();
            }
        }, 200);

        window.rhf_inView_event = setInterval(function () {
            if ( !window.RECS_rhfInView && $('#rhf_container').size() > 0) {
                rhfInView();
            }
        }, 200);
    } else {
        $(window).scroll(rhfShvlEventHandler);
        $(window).scroll(rhfInView);
    }

})($); }
if (window.rhf_use_AUI) {
    //Register a component
    P.when('jQuery', 'ready').register('rhf-bootstrapper', function($){
       return {
            bootstrap : function(){
                return rhfShovelerBootstrapFunction($);

       };

        rhfBootstrapper.bootstrap();

P.when("A").execute(function(A) {
   
   function vote(event) {
     var root = A.$(event.data.rootComponentId);
     var target = event.$target;
     root.find(".cr-vote-buttons").addClass("a-hidden");
     root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").removeClass("a-hidden");
       
     A.get(target.attr("href") + "&type=json&_=" + (new Date()).getTime(),
     {
	   dataType: 'json',
	   ajaxTimeout: 10000,
	   success: function(data, textStatus){ 
         success(data, root, target);
       },
	   error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
         error(root, target);
       }
	 });
     event.$event.preventDefault();

   }

   function isNoButton(target) {       
     return target.closest(".noButton").length > 0;
   }

   function success(data, root, target) {
       if (data.redirect == 1) {
	   window.location.href = target.attr("href");
       } else if (data.error == 1) {
	   error(root, target);
       } else {
	   if (isNoButton(target)) {
               root.find(".cr-vote-inapp").removeClass("a-hidden");
	   }
	   root.find(".cr-vote-success").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
	   root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
       }
   }

   function error(root, target) {
       root.find(".cr-vote-error").removeClass("a-hidden");	   
       root.find(".cr-vote-feedback").addClass("a-hidden");
   }

   A.declarative("cr-vote", ["click"], vote);
});
